 Maintain newness in relationship like this
 
 
 1
 Whether your relation is new or old, give personal space to your partner
 jis rishte main log apane partner par zyada pratibandh lagaate hai wo rishta zyada samay tak nahin chalata
 For healthy relation, it is necessary to spend time with your partner as much as it is necessary to give yourself time and also not to interfere in your partner's personal space
 aise jaaniye, kya he shaadi karne kaa sahi samay!2
 Share your day-long experience with a partner
 aapako unki koun si baat sabase zyada pasand he unhen bataaen
 Try to find out what your partner likes
 isse aap donon ke bich vishwaas badhegaa or imoshanalee aap ek duusare ke zyada kareeb aaenge
 3
 apane kariyar plan or lakshya ke bare main apane partner ko jarur bataaen
 Because every person in life has their dreams, goals
 aapako nai job ke liye shahar se baahar bhi janaa pad saktaa he
 Therefore, tell your partner clearly about your plan beforehand
 taaki aage jaakar aap donon ke rishte main koi samasya naa aae

 apane rishte kaa dayera bhi jarur tay karen
 Do discuss with your partner what you both like and what you don't
 aapako apane partner kii kis baat se sabase zyada dukh pahunch saktaa he
 Knowing and understanding everything about each other better does not cause bitterness in the relationship and also makes the relationship stronger

 china ke saath bharat ke vyapaar kaa ghaataa varsh 2015 main badhkar 51
 45 billion dollars
 " isamen kaha gaya, "dirghakaalik vyapaarik ghate vaale or bhugtan sambandhi samasyaon ke santulan kii samasya kaa saamana karne vaale desh ke taur par, bharat vyapaar ghaaton ko lekar hameshaa se satark rahaa he
 Therefore, Chinese products can easily hit the target of India's anti-dumping restrictions
 ' The article said that after the Indian Prime Minister Narendra Modi started promoting the 'make in India' slogan, some media and citizens of the country have seen a large number of China-made balloons, candles and jhalers appearing on Hindu festivals in large numbers
 Raised the issue fiercely
 unhone yah sawaal uthaaya, "kya hamaari keemtee videshi mudra ko in utpaadon par barbaad kiya janaa chahie? yaa "kya bhartiya utpaadan udyog in chizon ko bana paane main behad pichde hue hai?" The newspaper stated, "although reasonably priced attractive items are consumers' first choice
 iske alaava bhartiya media har samay jis vyapaarik maal kii baat karata he, vah china kii ore se bharat ko kiye jane vaale niryaaton kaa ek chota sa hissaa bhar he
 "it added," being a major exporter of high-tech goods, China today exports mainly high-technology products to India
 inamen electric upkaran, doorsanchaar upkaran, train locomotive, computer or telephone shaamil hai
 All these are necessary for the economic development of India and the daily life of its people

 This organization is accused of the January 2 Pathankot attack
 china ne bharat ke is kadam ko vifal karte hue ajahar ko sanyukt raashtra se pratibandhit karaane ke mudde par takneekee aadhaar par duusari baar adnga laga diya tha

 china or bharat ke sambandhon par seemaa vivaad or pakistan ke saath china ke sambandhon kii chaaya hameshaa se mandaraate rahane kii baat ko rekhaankit karte hue lekh main kaha gaya, ‘‘haalanki donon paksh kaaphi samay pehle hi yah samaj gaye the ki ek-duusare ke prati shatruta rakhane ke bajaay matbhedon ko darkinar kar dena donon ke samgr vikaas liye laabhadaayak he

 Not only this, it will also fail to bring about a fundamental change in India's existing trade relations with China
 antat: yah ek choti si ghatana se badhkar kuch nahin hoga
 "referring to the improvement in political relations between India and China since former Prime Minister Rajiv Gandhi's visit to China in 1988, the newspaper said that the economic and trade relations of the two countries have also received a boost, after which China since 2013 Has been India's largest trading partner
 isamen kaha gaya, "nishchit taur par, raajnneetik muddon se itar, kuch aarthik karkon ne bhi china or bharat ke vyapaarik vikaas ko baadhit kiya he
 Unresolved issues between the two countries often affect their mutual political trust and this results from non-tariff barriers against Chinese capital and products, such as security investigations of large projects in the sectors of defense, telecommunications, internet and transport
 Has emerged as " The newspaper said of the widening trade deficit, "on economic grounds, India's trade relations with China are unbalanced
 china ke saath badhata vyapaar ghaataa nayi dilli ko naaraaz kar rahaa he
 India's trade deficit with China increased to 51 in 2015
 45 arab dollar ho gaya
 "it added," As a country with long-term trade deficits and a balance of payments related problems, India has always been vigilant about trade deficits
 isliye chini utpaada aasaani se bharat ke damping-virdohi pratibandhon ke nishane par aa sakate hai
 ' lekh main kaha gaya ki bhartiya pradhanmantri narendra modi dwaara ‘mek in india’ naare ko badhaava die jane kii shuruuaat kiye jane par, desh ke kuch media or nagarikon ne hindu tyoharon par badi sankhya main najar aane vaale china nirmit gubbaaron, kandilon or jhaalaron ke mudde ko jamkar uthaaya
 He raised the question, "should our precious foreign exchange be wasted on these products?" Or "are Indian manufacturing industries extremely backward in making these things?" akhbaar ne kaha, "haalanki uchit keemat vaali aakshark chijen upabhoktaaon kii pehali pasand hoti he
 In addition, the merchandise that the Indian media talks about all the time is only a small part of the exports made by China to India
 " isamen kaha gaya, "ucch takneekee vastuon ke ek bade niryaatak hone ke naate, aaj china bharat ko mukhyat: ucch praudyogiki vaale utpaada niryaat karata he
 These include electric equipment, telecommunications equipment, train locomotives, computers, and telephones
 ye sabhi bharat ke aarthik vikaas or uski janata ke dainik jivan ke liye jaruri hai
 "comments akhbaar ne kaha, "kya bhartiya janata bahishkaar ke aahvaan kaa jawaab degi? yah abhiyaan kab tak chalegaa? bharat-china sambandhon par iskaa kya vishesh asar hoga? yahaan tak ki pratibandh kaa dabaav bana rahe bhartiya media ke paas bhi jawaab nahin hai

 ) chaatr jivan main hi aresas se jude rajnath singh ko ek baar phir sangh-bijepi ke takaraav kaa phayda mila
 Singh, who took charge of the bjp's national president for the third time, has taken charge of the Chief Minister of Uttar Pradesh and important ministries like surface transport, agriculture at the center and this time he has been removed as the chairman during the 2009 Lok Sabha elections
 In 2014, the party has the responsibility to reach power
 india today ke pramukh samvaadadatasantosh kumarase unhone party kii chunautiyon or bhavishya kii ranneeti par vistrut baatcheet kii
 Excerpts from this: What will be your priorities in the second innings as party president? Firstly to make the organizational structure active and effective, as well as to motivate the workers to resolve the issues of the general public where the government is and where it is not Struggle
 saath hi saath kaaryakartaaon kii vaicharik patibaddhtaayen bhi bade
 You shared the experience after stepping down from the post of president last time and said that activists should be committed to ideology in the same way as communists
 aapako thodi kami party main dikhi
 Now what steps will you take to overcome that deficiency, any concrete plan in your mind? Absolutely, there will be training camps
 uske madhyam se ham unka kamitment badhaane kii koshish karenge or 2013 ke vidhansabha or 2014 ke loksabhaa chunaav main bijepi ko jeet mili, ye hamaari koshish hogi
 But the biggest thing i want is that every worker of BJP should try to overcome this lack of faith in the general public towards politics, politicians and political systems
 yani uske kriti-kathan (vardes or dead) main antar nahin hona chahie
 What difference do you feel between the two terms? Since the first term was new, it took a year or two to understand the whole country
 uske baad loksabhaa kaa chunaav aa gaya
 But during this three years between which i was not the president, during this time i have got an experience of coming to the country
 main samajhataa hum ki uskaa laabh nishchit rup se is baar kaam karne main mujhe milegaa
 i would like to say one more thing that i will not try to run the party alone, i will run the party only with confidence
 aapane pichley turm main adhyaksh ke kaarykaal ko paanch saal yaa teen-teen saal ke do turm karne kii baat kii thi, lekin party or sangh taiyaar nahin hua
 This time the constitutional amendment for Gadkari fulfilled that desire of yours
 aisa nahin tha, kuch kanfusion rahaa he
 At that time, the Sangh Party was ready
 wo log usee samay turm badhaane ke liye taiyaar the, lekin maine hi apni ore se kaha tha ki party adhyaksh rahete apane antim varshon main apana kaarykaal badhaane ke liye samvidhan main sanshodhan nahin karuunga, nahin to ye massej jayega ki apana kaarykaal badhaane ke liye rajnath singh ne samvidhan main sanshodhan kar diya
 But did this happen in the last year for Gadkari? That was the offer i had made
 jab meraa turm badhaane kii baat ho rahi thi, to maine kaha tha ki aglaa jo bhi adhyaksh hoga uske turm ko badhaane kaa prastaav main hi pesh karuunga

 kya mukhyamantri sansadeey board main ho sakate hai, kyonki aapane pichley turm main yah daleel dete hue narendra modi ko board se hataaya tha ki siem ke bare main faisla sansadeey board karata he, isliye isamen siem nahin hone chahie?dekhie, daleel nahin di thi

 lekin meraa maananaa he ki ho sakate hai

 to kya aapaki team main modi yaa koi siem sansadeey board main ho sakate hai?is sambhaavna ko nakaara nahin ja saktaa he

 kya party ke purv adhyaksh ke faisle kii samiksha hogi yaa aap bhi unke rukh se sahamat he?dekhie, mere upar nai jimmedaari ai he
 i will call a meeting of the Parliamentary Board and decide in it
 kya aap loksabhaa chunaav se pehle cheharaa project karne ke paksh main hai?dekhie, main adhyaksh hum or main apni koi nijee raay nahin rakh saktaa varna iskaa massej galat jayega
 Whatever decision will be taken in this regard, only the Parliamentary Board will do it
 narendra modi ko lekar party main kaaphi josh dikh rahaa he, yashavanth sinha or yahaan tak ki sangh parivaar se ashok singhl sareekhe kai netaaon ne khulkar unhen project karne kii pairvi kii he, kya party unke naam par vichaar karegi?desh main narendra modi ko lekar josh he, isamen koi andeh nahin
 Narendra Modi is our most popular leader and i am very happy that leaders like Modi are with us, who are excited about it
